==============================
Table A6. Panel 2SLS Estimates of Malaria Impact on TFP using Combined instruments 
==============================


Call:
ivreg::ivreg(formula = tfp_log ~ case_incidence_log + agr_share_log + 
    trade_openness_log + cpi_log + edu_log + factor(Country.Name) | 
    hbs_olr_o + lag_case_incidence_log + log(olr_o) + agr_share_log +
